<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:недостача.html>недоста́ча</a> (26072)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">недоста́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nedostátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ча</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ča</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:недостижимый.html>недостижи́мый</a> (17421)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">достижи́мый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dostižímyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недостижимый.html>недостижи́мый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nedostižímyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)недостижи́мее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)недостижи́мей</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:недостижимый.html>недостижи́мый</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:недостойный.html>недосто́йный</a> (7574)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:достойный.html>досто́йный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dostójnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недостойный.html>недосто́йный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nedostójnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>unworthy <i>(of)</i></li>
<li>unworthy, disreputable, dishonourable, contemptible, unbecoming

***недотрога.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:недотрога.html>недотро́га</a> (32018)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">not</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">дотро́г-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dotróg-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">touch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-a</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The botany term is a calque of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">Impatiens noli-tangere</i>; cf. <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">не-тронь-меня́</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ne-tronʹ-menjá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недотрога.html>недотро́га</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nedotróga</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недотрога.html>недотро́ги</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недотрога.html>недотро́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недотрога.html>недотро́г</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li class="senseid" id="Russian-touchy_person"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> touchy person, touch-me-not</li>
<li class="senseid" id="Russian-plant"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> touch-me-not</li></ol>

***недоумевать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:недоумевать.html>недоумева́ть</a> (7439)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">недо-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nedo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уметь.html>уме́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">umétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недоумевать.html>недоумева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nedoumevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to be at a loss, to be bewildered, to be puzzled, to be perplexed</li></ol>

***недоумение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:недоумение.html>недоуме́ние</a> (3581)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недоумение.html>недоуме́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nedouménije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недоумение.html>недоуме́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недоумение.html>недоуме́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недоумение.html>недоуме́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bewilderment, perplexity, quandary (a state of not knowing what to decide)</li></ol>

***недра.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:недра.html>не́дра</a> (6530)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nědra</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недра.html>не́дра</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nédra</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недра.html>не́др</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rare</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> womb</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rare</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bosom</li>
<li>subsoil, bowels of the earth</li></ol>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:впрочем.html>Впро́чем</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:барышня.html>ба́рышню</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:находить.html>находи́ла</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>ей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ботинок.html>боти́нки</a>. — <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:недурно.html>Недурно</a></span>… <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:недурно.html>недурно</a></span>… — <a href = vnd.unilang:любоваться.html>любу́ется</a> Евгения. — <a href = vnd.unilang:правда.html>Правда</a>, <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:недурно.html>недурно</a></span>, Николай? <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>О</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеться.html>хоте́лось</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ответить.html>отве́тить</a>: — <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>Нет</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:скверный.html>скве́рно</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>Тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сорок.html>сорок</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a>. </span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нежели.html>не́жели</a> (5292)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нежели.html>не́жели</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">néželi</span>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> than</li></ol>

***нежить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нежить.html>не́жить</a> (20621)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нега.html>не́га</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">néga</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нежить.html>не́жить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">néžitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>

<ol><li>to pamper</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нежный.html>не́жный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">néžnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>жить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нежить.html>не́жить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">néžitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нежить.html>не́жити</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нежить.html>не́жити</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нежить.html>не́житей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> mythology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> evil or dangerous spirits in Slavic mythology</li>

***нежно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нежный.html>не́жно</a> (3952)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нежный.html>не́жный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">néžnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нежный.html>не́жно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">néžno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>dearly, fondly, gently</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нежный.html>не́жно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">néžno</span>)
</p>
